general 2022-09-22 22:02:55 orangutans are a species of great apes native to the islands of borneo and sumatra. the majority of orangutans live on borneo. there are 3 species of orangutans, the bornean orangutan (most common) the sumatran orangutan (coolest) and the tapanuli orangutan (these are not real!). orangutans mostly eat fruit but they also eat small insects. orangutans are the largest tree dwelling mammal in the world. the average orangutan is 4 foot 11 inches tall, and their armspan is 7 foot long! thats almost as big as me. 
orangutans are highly intelligent and are capable of recognizing themselves in mirrors, use tools, and wash themselves off. orangutan babies stay with their mothers for 7 years, to teach the baby orangutan how to live in the dense jungles of borneo and sumatra. there are 100,000 bornean orangutans, 6000 sumatran orangutans and roughly 800 tapanuli orangutans in the world. the main threat to orangutans is habitat loss, and palm oil production. 2000 to 3000 orangutans are die each year because of this  all species of orangutans are classified as critically endangered (sad music playing with sad orangutans) . On the bright side there are many organizations that are helping the conservation of orangutans!
